123.2(1): med pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can rnams/ nyon mongs 
123.3(1): pa gti mug gi mtshan ma rang sar grol nas/ me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi don rtogs 
123.4(1): te longs spyod rdzogs sku'i klong du sangs rgyas par gyur cig /ces gdab bo/ /pho 
123.5(1): brang yid 'ong gzhal yas kyi/ bder gshegs kun rig lha tshogs rnams/ ye nas 
123.6(1): mnyam nyid dag pa la/ sku khrus gsol lta mi 'tshal te/ bdag dang mtha' yas 
123.7(1): sems can rnams/ ma rtogs nga rgyal sgrib pa can/ nga rgyal sgrib pa dag bya'i phyir/
123.8(1): gtsang ma'i sku khrus 'di gsol bas/ nga rgyal nyon mongs dag gyur cig /bswo A+o~M na 
123.9(1): ma ting nam gu shud d+he sale sange ye swahA/ bum pa zlum po ngo bo nyid kyi sku/ ngang la 
123.10(1): ma g.yos ma bcos mnyam pa nyid/ skal ldan skyes bu rnams la dbang bskur bas/

123.14(1): mtha' yas sems can rnams/ nyon mongs pa nga rgyal gyi mtshan ma thams cad rang 
123.15(1): sar grol nas/ mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi don rtogs te/ ngo bo nyid sku'i klong du 
123.16(1): sangs rgyas par gyur cig /ces gdab bo/ pho brang yid 'ong gzhal yas kyi/ bder 
123.17(1): gshegs kun rig lha tshogs rnams/ ye nas sor rtogs dag pa la/ sku khrus gsol 
123.18(1): lta mi 'tshal te/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can rnams/ ma rtogs 'dod chags

427.2(1): gshis/ 'dir bon gyi gzhung lugs ngo ma shes 'dod na bon gyi gsung rab dpe cha 'di 
427.3(1): lta bu la blta klog dang zhib 'jug gnang re'i ched dang / g.yung drung bon gyi bla sprul 
427.4(1): mkhas dbang mang pos yun ring re bskul byas pa'i rkyen dang / rgya che'i bod yig klog 
427.5(1): pa po yongs la blta bde 'khyer sla'i cha rkyen du dmigs nas/ ston pa'i gsung rab lung 
427.6(1): gi bon rin po che'i skor deb phreng brgya dang lnga bcu can zhig yig dkar gyi lam nas 
427.7(1): legs bsgrigs byas te/ rje smra seng bla ma'i gsung gi byin rlabs las 'phos pa/ g.yung 
427.8(1): drung bon gyi rgyud gzhung rin po che'i khrod kyi thun mong min pa'i brda chad/[ <<]gsung rab 
427.9(1): sgo mdzod rin po che'i glegs bam[>>]zhes pa dpe tshogs spyi chings kyi mtshan du gsol nas 
427.10(1): dpar 'grems zhus pa yin/
427.11(1): zhus dag thad las rim dngos la thog ma'i ma dpe gang la byas pa/ bar du dpe cha 
427.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
427.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
427.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2011lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
427.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
427.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
427.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
427.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
427.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
427.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
427.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
427.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
428.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
428.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
428.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
428.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
428.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
428.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
428.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
428.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
428.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
428.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
428.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
428.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
428.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
428.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
428.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
428.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
428.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
428.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
428.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi 
428.20(1): ma 'gro kun yongs la shar ba'i smon 'dun dang bcas 'byung ldan 301 spyi lo 2015 5[ / ]1
428.21(1): nyin/ g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang nas bris/ /
